<userid>107420538524913884106</userid>< username>
YESSENIA GARCIA</username>

<pictures>None</pictures></record></dataset><record>
< text>
This was the second time I'd taken my car to Legit Automotive. The first time, they fixed an existing problem and made me aware of something else they found, which "I would need to fix sooner or later if I was going to keep the car". Well, about six months went by, and sure enough that time eventually came. It was an involved and complicated repair. When I showed up to get the car, Gary had saved the parts to show me exactly what they did, the components that had gone bad, and how they replaced it, and additional problems they found that needed to be fixed as they related to the existing repair/issue. They were fully transparent about parts and labor, and the price for the job was very fair based upon what I was quoted by other mechanics. Also, the interior of my car was clean when I picked it up despite being worked on for many hours.
